as a middleware-based system that intercepts query and resource requests at the plugin backend level. The architecture comprises several key components:\\n\\n### 1. Cache Middleware (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/caching_middleware.go`)\\nThe `CachingMiddleware` class implements `backend.HandlerMiddleware` and intercepts both `QueryData()` and `CallResource()` requests. For each request:\\n- It calls `HandleQueryRequest()` to check if results are cached\\n- On cache hit, returns cached response immediately\\n- On cache miss, executes the actual query and calls `UpdateCacheFn()` to store results\\n- Integrates request deduplication to prevent duplicate concurrent requests\\n- Records cache performance metrics (hit/miss rates, request duration)\\n\\n### 2. Cache Key Generation (`pkg/services/caching/service.go`)\\nThe `GetKey()` function generates cache keys from query requests:\\n- Uses `JSONEncoder` to serialize the entire query request to JSON\\n- Applies SHA256 hashing via `SHA256KeyFunc()` to create a deterministic, fixed-length key\\n- Prefixes the key with the datasource UID to isolate caches per datasource\\n- Format: `{dataSourceUID}:{sha256_hash}`\\n\\n### 3. Cache Service Interface (`pkg/services/caching/service.go`)\\nThe `CachingService` interface defines two core methods:\\n- `HandleQueryRequest()`: Checks cache and returns `CachedQueryDataResponse` with optional update function\\n- `HandleResourceRequest()`: Similar pattern for HTTP resource requests\\n- The OSS implementation (`OSSCachingService`) is a no-op that always returns cache misses (caching is an enterprise feature)\\n\\n### 4. Cache Backend Abstraction (`pkg/infra/remotecache/remotecache.go`)\\nThe `RemoteCache` class provides unified access to different cache backends via the `CacheStorage` interface:\\n\\n**Supported Backends:**\\n- **Redis** (`pkg/infra/remotecache/redis_storage.go`): Uses go-redis client, supports TLS, password auth, connection pooling\\n- **Memcached** (`pkg/infra/remotecache/memcached_storage.go`): Uses gomemcache client\\n- **Database** (`pkg/infra/remotecache/database_storage.go`): Stores in `cache_data` SQL table with garbage collection every 10 minutes\\n\\nThe `RemoteCache` wrapper class applies optional decoration layers:\\n- **Encryption Wrapper** (`encryptedCacheStorage`): Encrypts cached values using the secrets service\\n- **Prefix Wrapper** (`prefixCacheStorage`): Adds a configured prefix to all cache keys for namespace isolation\\n\\n### 5. Cache Configuration (`pkg/setting/setting_remote_cache.go`)\\nThe `RemoteCacheSettings` struct configures cache behavior:\\n- `Name`: Cache type (\\\"redis\\\", \\\"memcached\\\", or \\\"database\\\")\\n- `ConnStr`: Connection string for Redis/Memcached\\n- `Prefix`: Optional key prefix for namespace isolation\\n- `Encryption`: Boolean flag to enable encryption of cached values\\n- Default TTL is 24 hours (configured in `defaultMaxCacheExpiration` in remotecache.go)\\n- Per-query TTL can be overridden via datasource configuration\\n\\n### 6. Cache Metrics (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/caching_metrics.go`)\\nPrometheus histograms track cache performance:\\n- `grafana_caching_query_caching_request_duration_seconds`: Query cache request latency\\n- `grafana_caching_resource_caching_request_duration_seconds`: Resource cache request latency\\n- `grafana_caching_should_cache_query_request_duration_seconds`: Time spent evaluating whether to cache (AWS async queries)\\n\\n### 7. Request Deduplication Middleware\\nThe `requestDeduplicationMiddleware` prevents duplicate concurrent requests using Go's `singleflight.Group`:\\n- When N requests execute the same query simultaneously, only 1 query executes\\n- Other N-1 requests wait for the first result and use the same response\\n- Cache key is derived from datasource UID and query request\\n\\n### Cache Invalidation Strategy\\nThe cache relies on:\\n1. **TTL-based expiration**: Cache entries expire after their configured TTL (default 24h, configurable per datasource)\\n2. **Explicit deletion**: Individual cache entries can be deleted via `RemoteCache.Delete()` (used when secrets change, etc.)\\n3. **Database GC**: For database backend, expired entries are cleaned up every 10 minutes by `databaseCache.internalRunGC()`\\n\\nNote: Cache invalidation on dashboard save is not explicitly implemented via hooks. Instead, the caching operates at the query execution level - dashboard changes don't automatically invalidate; queries return cached results until expiration. This is the enterprise caching feature design.\\n\\n### Enterprise vs OSS\\n- **OSS**: `OSSCachingService` is always used, which returns cache misses (no-op)\\n- **Enterprise**: Enterprise caching service implementations would be provided that actually use the `RemoteCache` backend\\n\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":524,"cache_read_input_tokens":115981,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":524},"output_tokens":6,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"0ed9274d-5b41-48b8-b0ec-92a43f3b27e2","uuid":"2436d375-5370-4a56-be6c-9e6d4cb61dbc"}

as a middleware-based system that intercepts query and resource requests at the plugin backend level. The architecture comprises several key components:\\n\\n### 1. Cache Middleware (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/caching_middleware.go`)\\nThe `CachingMiddleware` class implements `backend.HandlerMiddleware` and intercepts both `QueryData()` and `CallResource()` requests. For each request:\\n- It calls `HandleQueryRequest()` to check if results are cached\\n- On cache hit, returns cached response immediately\\n- On cache miss, executes the actual query and calls `UpdateCacheFn()` to store results\\n- Integrates request deduplication to prevent duplicate concurrent requests\\n- Records cache performance metrics (hit/miss rates, request duration)\\n\\n### 2. Cache Key Generation (`pkg/services/caching/service.go`)\\nThe `GetKey()` function generates cache keys from query requests:\\n- Uses `JSONEncoder` to serialize the entire query request to JSON\\n- Applies SHA256 hashing via `SHA256KeyFunc()` to create a deterministic, fixed-length key\\n- Prefixes the key with the datasource UID to isolate caches per datasource\\n- Format: `{dataSourceUID}:{sha256_hash}`\\n\\n### 3. Cache Service Interface (`pkg/services/caching/service.go`)\\nThe `CachingService` interface defines two core methods:\\n- `HandleQueryRequest()`: Checks cache and returns `CachedQueryDataResponse` with optional update function\\n- `HandleResourceRequest()`: Similar pattern for HTTP resource requests\\n- The OSS implementation (`OSSCachingService`) is a no-op that always returns cache misses (caching is an enterprise feature)\\n\\n### 4. Cache Backend Abstraction (`pkg/infra/remotecache/remotecache.go`)\\nThe `RemoteCache` class provides unified access to different cache backends via the `CacheStorage` interface:\\n\\n**Supported Backends:**\\n- **Redis** (`pkg/infra/remotecache/redis_storage.go`): Uses go-redis client, supports TLS, password auth, connection pooling\\n- **Memcached** (`pkg/infra/remotecache/memcached_storage.go`): Uses gomemcache client\\n- **Database** (`pkg/infra/remotecache/database_storage.go`): Stores in `cache_data` SQL table with garbage collection every 10 minutes\\n\\nThe `RemoteCache` wrapper class applies optional decoration layers:\\n- **Encryption Wrapper** (`encryptedCacheStorage`): Encrypts cached values using the secrets service\\n- **Prefix Wrapper** (`prefixCacheStorage`): Adds a configured prefix to all cache keys for namespace isolation\\n\\n### 5. Cache Configuration (`pkg/setting/setting_remote_cache.go`)\\nThe `RemoteCacheSettings` struct configures cache behavior:\\n- `Name`: Cache type (\\\"redis\\\", \\\"memcached\\\", or \\\"database\\\")\\n- `ConnStr`: Connection string for Redis/Memcached\\n- `Prefix`: Optional key prefix for namespace isolation\\n- `Encryption`: Boolean flag to enable encryption of cached values\\n- Default TTL is 24 hours (configured in `defaultMaxCacheExpiration` in remotecache.go)\\n- Per-query TTL can be overridden via datasource configuration\\n\\n### 6. Cache Metrics (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/caching_metrics.go`)\\nPrometheus histograms track cache performance:\\n- `grafana_caching_query_caching_request_duration_seconds`: Query cache request latency\\n- `grafana_caching_resource_caching_request_duration_seconds`: Resource cache request latency\\n- `grafana_caching_should_cache_query_request_duration_seconds`: Time spent evaluating whether to cache (AWS async queries)\\n\\n### 7. Request Deduplication Middleware\\nThe `requestDeduplicationMiddleware` prevents duplicate concurrent requests using Go's `singleflight.Group`:\\n- When N requests execute the same query simultaneously, only 1 query executes\\n- Other N-1 requests wait for the first result and use the same response\\n- Cache key is derived from datasource UID and query request\\n\\n### Cache Invalidation Strategy\\nThe cache relies on:\\n1. **TTL-based expiration**: Cache entries expire after their configured TTL (default 24h, configurable per datasource)\\n2. **Explicit deletion**: Individual cache entries can be deleted via `RemoteCache.Delete()` (used when secrets change, etc.)\\n3. **Database GC**: For database backend, expired entries are cleaned up every 10 minutes by `databaseCache.internalRunGC()`\\n\\nNote: Cache invalidation on dashboard save is not explicitly implemented via hooks. Instead, the caching operates at the query execution level - dashboard changes don't automatically invalidate; queries return cached results until expiration. This is the enterprise caching feature design.\\n\\n### Enterprise vs OSS\\n- **OSS**: `OSSCachingService` is always used, which returns cache misses (no-op)\\n- **Enterprise**: Enterprise caching service implementations would be provided that actually use the `RemoteCache` backend\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
